				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Pièces d'orgue, Livre 1 (Dandrieu, Jean-François)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="wp_header">
<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>63 Pieces divided into 6 Suites, each containing an <i>Offertoire</i>, various pieces and a complete <i>Magnificat</i>.
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Publication
</th>
<td>1739 (Posthumous)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>
<td><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Pieces&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Pieces</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:For_organ&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">For organ</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Scores_featuring_the_organ&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Scores featuring the organ</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:For_1_player&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">For 1 player</a></span>
</td></tr></table>

<h4> <span class="mw-headline" id="Suite_IV._Pi.C3.A8ces_en_G._R.C3.A9_Sol_majeur">Suite IV. Pièces en G. Ré Sol majeur</span></h4>

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Premier Livre de Pièces d'Orgue
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Dandrieu,_Jean-Fran%C3%A7ois" title="Category:Dandrieu, Jean-François">Dandrieu, Jean-François</a>
</td></tr>
<tr class="udelonly" data-display="table-row">
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>None <small>[<span class="icatassign">force assignment</span>]</small>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>63 Pieces divided into 6 Suites, each containing an <i>Offertoire</i>, various pieces and a complete <i>Magnificat</i>.
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Pub<span class="mh555">lication</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1739 (Posthumous)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Composer Time Period</span><span class="ms555">Comp. Period</span>
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Baroque" title="Category:Baroque">Baroque</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Piece Style
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Baroque_style" title="Category:Baroque style">Baroque</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Instrumentation
</th>
<td>Organ
</td></tr></table>
</div>
<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="Misc._Comments">Misc. Comments</span></h2>
<p>Dandrieu died before completing the second organ book to which he referred in his <i>Avertissement</i> to the 1st book&#160;: «&#160;À l’égard du Second Livre que je me propose de publier dans la suite, il renfermera les autres Tons les plus en usage, traités d’une manière conforme à celle qu’on a suivie dans celui-ci.&#160;»
</p>
